[30;1m8 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m75 | [0m[35m### Cancel a worker Task and explicitly abort jobs after timeout[0m

[30;1m20 | [0m[35mInternally, each worker is responsible for ensuring that each periodic task is deferred[0m
[30;1m21 | [0m[35min time, and the database is responsible for making sure deferring only happens once per[0m
[30;1m22 | [0m[35mperiod, even with multiple workers. This means that you can have high availability[0m
[30;1m23 | [0m[35mperiodic scheduling: as long as at least one worker is up, the tasks will be deferred.[0m

[30;1m6 | [0m[35m## From the code[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35mIf a job is configured with a date in the future, it will run at the[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35mfirst opportunity after that date. Let's launch the task that will[0m
